kern

The font has GPOS kerning.

kern

-/-

Check if 'kern' table in font.

Font has no 'kern' table. Please verify if font requires kern table or if only GPOS kerning should be in font.

gasp Table

gasp Table

Pass

Unna Regular (Unna-Regular.ttf)

gasp

Version

Info

Unna Regular (Unna-Regular.ttf)

gasp

Default

Pull gasp table Default.

Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True

Pass

Unna Regular (Unna-Regular.ttf)

gasp

Default

Check gasp table Default.

gasp table default is:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True
and should be:
